<script type="text/javascript"> 
// Cache the elements we'll need
var menu = $('#cssmenu');
var menuList = menu.find('ul:first');
var listItems = menu.find('li').not('#responsive-tab');

// Create responsive trigger
menuList.prepend('<li id="responsive-tab"><a href="#">Menu</a></li>');

// Toggle menu visibility
menu.on('click', '#responsive-tab', function(){
	listItems.slideToggle('fast');
	listItems.addClass('collapsed');
});
this.tooltip = function(){	
	/* CONFIG */		
		xOffset = 10;
		yOffset = 20;		
		// these 2 variable determine popup's distance from the cursor
		// you might want to adjust to get the right result		
	/* END CONFIG */		
	$("a.tooltip").hover(function(e){											  
		this.t = this.title;
		this.title = "";									  
		$("body").append("<p id='tooltip'>"+ this.t +"</p>");
		$("#tooltip")
			.css("top",(e.pageY - xOffset) + "px")
			.css("left",(e.pageX + yOffset) + "px")
			.fadeIn("slow");		
    },
	function(){
		this.title = this.t;		
		$("#tooltip").remove();
    });	
	$("a.tooltip").mousemove(function(e){
		$("#tooltip")
			.css("top",(e.pageY - xOffset) + "px")
			.css("left",(e.pageX + yOffset) + "px");
	});	

};

// starting the script on page load
$(document).ready(function(){
	tooltip();
});
function showPic(name) { 
	file = "images/pets/" + name + ".png";
	document.getElementById("pics").innerHTML = "<img src='" + file + "' align=absmiddle>"; 
} 
function showPic2(name) { 
	file = "images/pets/" + name + ".png";
	document.getElementById("pics2").innerHTML = "<img src='" + file + "' align=absmiddle width=75>"; 
} 
function tools(){ 
var top=$ (document).scrollTop(); 
if(($.browser.msie==true)&&($.browser.version==6.0)){ 
if(top>200)$("#box1_1").css({ position:"absolute",top:top-200}); 
}else{ 
if(top>200)$("#box1_1").css({position:"fixed",top:"-"&top+"px"} ); 
} 
if(top<=200)$("#box1_1").css({position:"static",top:0}); 
} 
$(function(){ 
window.onscroll=tools; 
window.onresize= tools; 
}); 
$(function() {
	$(window).scroll(function() {
		if($(this).scrollTop() != 0) {
			$('#toTop').fadeIn();	
		} else {
			$('#toTop').fadeOut();
		}
	});
 
	$('#toTop').click(function() {
		$('body,html').animate({scrollTop:0},800);
	});	
});
</script>

function toggleMenu()
{
var elements = document.getElementsByClassName('ShowMonstersLv');
for(var i=0; i<elements.length; i++) { 
  elements[i].style.display= (elements[i].style.display=='block') ? 'none' : 'block';
}

}
</script>
